FACILITY   (CCW,2JPNOSA) Intense 14 MeV neutron source OKTAVIAN   2276600100014 
INC-SOURCE (D-T) 2 cm in diameter tritium target. Less than 2 ns  2276600100015 
            pulsed neutrons were generated                        2276600100016 
METHOD     (TOF) Flight path of ~8.3 m fixed at 85 deg.           2276600100017 
           (PSD) Two parallel pulse shape discrimination circuits 2276600100018 
            for separation of neutron signals from gamma signals. 2276600100019 
DETECTOR   (SCIN ) NE-213 liquid scintillator (25.4 cm in diam.,  2276600100020 
             10 cm in length).                                    2276600100021 
            The other NE-213 scintillator (5.08 cm diam., 5.08 cm 2276600100022 
             in length) for source neutron flux was monitor at    2276600100023 
             0 deg against the deuteron beam line.                2276600100024 
SAMPLE      Cylindrical samples of different sizes.               2276600100025 
CORRECTION  Corrections are made for                              2276600100026 
             - multiple scattering;                               2276600100027 
             - attenuation;                                       2276600100028 
             - neutron source contamination.                      2276600100029 
             with the help of MUSCC3 code based on JENDL-3.       2276600100030 
            In case that JENDL-3 would produce double             2276600100031 
             differential neutron emission spectrum in drastic    2276600100032 
             disagreement with the measured one, the correction   2276600100033 
             can be skipped and the adoption of raw (i.e.         2276600100034 
             experimental) data is recommended by authors.        2276600100035 
            This correction amounted to about 10% except for      2276600100036 
             backward elastic scattering where it could be up to  2276600100037 
             30%.                                                 2276600100038 
COMMENT    By authors:                                            2276600100039 
            Correction factor are calculated using evaluated data,2276600100040 
             however, they are still primitive.                   2276600100041 
            Calculation of correction factors should be carried   2276600100042 
             out again after new version of evaluation would be   2276600100043 
             published.                                           2276600100044
